breaks into tasks\n  ↓\nexecution_engine/integrated_form_executor.py (IntegratedFormExecutor)\n  ↓\nexecution_engine/task_executor.py (TaskExecutor)\n```\n\n### Flow 2: Confidence Validation\n```\nTask ready to execute\n  ↓\nconfidence_engine/unified_confidence_engine.py (UnifiedConfidenceEngine)\n  ↓\nconfidence_engine/murphy_gate.py (MurphyGate) - Connects corrections to learning\n   - Uses: CorrectionCapture, PatternExtraction, TrainingPipeline\n\n## WHAT\'S CONNECTED ✅\n\n- ✅ Form intake → Execution engine\n- ✅ Confidence engine → Murphy gate\n- ✅ Supervisor → HITL monitor\n- ✅ Corrections → Learning engine\n- ✅ Learning → Shadow agent\n\n## WHAT\'S MISSING ❌\n\n### 1. Create Session\n```bash\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/session/create \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{"user_id": "user123", "repository_id": "repo_1234567890"}\'\n```\n\nResponse: `{"success": true, "session_id": "session_1234567890"}`\n\n### 3. Send Message (Main Flow)\n```bash\ncurl -X POST http://localhost:5000/api/conversation/message \\\n  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \\\n  -d \'{\n    "message": "Automate my blog publishing to WordPress and Medium",\n    "session_id": "session_1234567890"\n  }\'\n```\n\nResponse:\n```json\n{\n  "success": true,\n  "intent": "automation_request",\n  "confidence": {"G": 0.85, "D": 0.90, "H": 0.95},\n  "gate_result": {"action": "PROCEED", "confidence": 0.90},\n  "execution": {"status": "completed", "tasks": [...]},\n  "agents": ["agent_1", "agent_2", "agent_3"]\n}\n```\n\n### 4. Check Conversation History\n```bash\ncurl http://localhost:5000/api/conversation/thread/session_1234567890\n```\n\n### 5. View Active Agents\n```bash\ncurl http://localhost:5000/api/swarm/agents?session_id=session_1234567890\n```\n\n### 6. Get Learning Patterns\n```bash\ncurl http://localhost:5000/api/learning/patterns\n```\n\n## What Happens Behind the Scenes\n\nWhen you send a message via `/api/conversation/message`:\n\n1. **Message Pipeline** - Processes and classifies intent\n2. **Domain Detection** - Determines domain (software, business, etc.)\n3. **Swarm Spawning** - Creates appropriate agent swarm\n4. **MFGC Orchestration** - Coordinates agent actions\n5. **Agent Collaboration** - Agents work together in workspace\n6. **Confidence Validation** - Calculates confidence scores\n7. **Murphy Gate** - Validates against thresholds\n8. **Execution** - Runs approved actions\n9. **Telemetry Capture** - Records execution data\n10. **Learning** - Improves from execution\n\n## System Architecture\n\n```\nUser Input\n  ↓\nmurphy_final_runtime.py (RuntimeOrchestrator)\n  ↓\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│  Message Pipeline → Intent Classifier   │\n│  Domain Detector → Swarm Spawner        │\n│  MFGC Controller → Agent Coordination   │\n│  Confidence Engine → Murphy Gate        │\n│  Execution Engine → Task Execution      │\n│  Telemetry → Learning → Improvement     │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────┘\n  ↓\nResponse to User\n```\n\n## Integration with murphy_ui_final.html\n\nUpdate the UI to use this runtime:\n\n```javascript\nconst API_BASE = \'http://localhost:5000\';\n\n// Create session on load\nfetch(`${API_BASE}/api/session/create`, {\n  method: \'POST\',\n  headers: {\'Content-Type\': \'application/json\'},\n  body: {\n  fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/conversation/message`, {\n    method: \'POST\',\n    headers: {\'Content-Type\': \'application/json\'},\n    body: JSON.stringify({message: message, session_id:    \n    def _extract_schedule(self, request: str) -> str:\n        """Extract schedule"""\n        if \'daily\' in request.lower():\n            return \'daily\'\n        if \'weekly\' in self._discover_platform_apis(info.get(\'platforms\', [])),\n            \'content_policies\': self._discover_content_policies(info.get(\'platforms\', [])),\n            \'legal_requirements\':   \'auth\': \'oauth\',\n                    \'docs\': \'https://developer.wordpress.org/rest-api/\'\n                }\n            elif platform == \'medium\':\n                apis[\'medium\'] = {\n Operational constraints (error handling, monitoring)\n    """\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.constraints = {}\n        \n    def compile(self, info: Dict[str, Any], regulations: Dict[str, \'business\': self._compile_business(info),\n            \'legal\': self._compile_legal(regulations),\n            \'operational\': self._compile_operational(regulations)\n        }\n        \n        self.constraints = constraints\n        return constraints\n        \n    def _compile_technical(self, regulations: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Compile technical constraints"""\n        return {\n            \'rate_limits\': regulations.get(\'platform_apis\', {}),\n            \'timeouts\': regulations.get(\'technical_constraints\', {}).get(\'timeout\', 30),\n            \'max_retries\': regulations.get(\'technical_constraints\', {}).get(\'max_retries\', 3)\n        }\n        \n    def _compile_business(self, info: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Compile business constraints"""\n        return {\n            \'approval_required\': info.get(\'approval_required\', False),\n            \'quality_threshold\': 0.8,\n            \'schedule\': info.get(\'schedule\', \'manual\')\n        }\n        \n    def _compile_legal(self, regulations: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Compile legal constraints"""\n        return regulations.get(\'legal_requirements\', {})\n        \n    def _compile_operational(self, regulations: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Compile operational constraints"""\n        return }\n\nclass AgentGenerator:\n    """\n    Generates agents from templates + constraints\n    - Takes domain swarm template\n    - Applies discovered constraints\n    - Creates configured agents ready to execute\n    """\n    def __init__(self):\n        self.generated_agents = []\n        \n    def generate(self, domain: str, info: Dict[str, Any], constraints: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Dict[str, self._get_domain_template(domain)\n        \n        # Generate agents from template\n        for agent_spec in template:\n            agent = self._create_agent(agent_spec, info, constraints)\n            agents.append(agent)\n            \n        self.generated_agents = agents\n        return agents\n        \n    def _get_domain_template(self, domain: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n }\n\nclass SandboxManager:\n    """\n    Manages sandbox environments for automation execution\n    - Creates isolated environments\n    - Installs dependencies\n    - Manages credentials\n    - Sets self._setup_credentials(agents),\n            \'output_dir\': self._create_output_dir(automation_id)\n        }\n        \n        self.sandboxes[automation_id] = sandbox\n        return sandbox\n        \n    def _create_environment(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Create isolated environment"""\n        return {\n            \'type\': \'docker\',\n            \'image\': \'murphy-runtime:latest\',\n            \'isolated\': True\n        }\n        \n    def _install_dependencies(self, agents: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> List[str]:\n        """Install required dependencies"""\n        deps = set()\n        for agent in agents:\n            if agent[\'type\'] == \'Publisher\':\n                deps.add(\'wordpress-api\')\n __init__(self):\n        self.info_gatherer = InformationGatheringAgent()\n        self.regulation_discoverer = RegulationDiscoveryAgent()\n        self.constraint_compiler = ConstraintCompiler()\n        self.agent_generator = AgentGenerator()\n        self.sandbox_manager = SandboxManager()\n        \n    def execute_phase1(self, request: str, domain: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """\n        Execute Phase 1: Generative Setup\n        """\n        logger.info("=" * 60)\n        logger.info("PHASE 1: GENERATIVE SETUP")\n        logger.info("=" * 60)\n        \n        # 1. Discover regulations\n        logger.info("2. Discovering regulations...")\n        regulations = self.regulation_discoverer.discover(info)\n        logger.info(f"   Regulations: {len(regulations)} categories")\n        \n        # 3. Compile constraints\n        logger.info("3. Compiling constraints...")\n        constraints = self.constraint_compiler.compile(info, regulations)\n        logger.info(f"   Constraints: {len(constraints)} categories")\n        \n        # 4. Generate agents\n        logger.info("4. Generating agents...")\n        agents = self.agent_generator.generate(domain, info, constraints)\n        logger.info(f"   Generated: {len(agents)} agents")\n        \n        # 5. Setup sandbox\n        automation_id = f"auto_{datetime.now().timestamp()}"\n        logger.info(f"5. Execute workflow\n        logger.info("2. Executing workflow...")\n        results = self._execute_workflow(config)\n        logger.info(f"   Execution: {results[\'status\']}")\n        \n        # 3. Produce deliverables\n        logger.info("3. Analyze Request\nanalysis = {\n    \'type\': \'factory_automation\',\n    \'domain\': \'hvac_control\',\n    \'actions_needed\': [\'READ_SENSOR\', \'WRITE_ACTUATOR\']\n}\n\n# 2. Compile ExecutionPacket\npacket = PacketCompiler.compile(\n    actions=[\n        Action(\n            action_type=ActionType.READ_SENSOR,\n            parameters={\'sensor_id\': \'temp_sensor_1\', \'protocol\': \'Modbus\'}\n        ),\n        Action(\n            action_type=ActionType.WRITE_ACTUATOR,\n            parameters={\'actuator_id\': \'hvac_unit_1\', \'protocol\': \'BACnet\'}\n        )\n    ],\n    constraints=constraints,\n    gates=[\n        Gate(\n            gate_id=\'safety_check\',\n            predicate=\'temperature >= 55 and temperature <= 85\'\n        )\n    ]\n)\n\n# 6. Create Session (With ONLY selected engines)\nsession = SessionManager.create_session(\n    user_id=\'factory_manager\',\n    repository_id=\'factory_hvac\',\n    engines=engines,\n    packet=packet\n)\n```\n\n### Phase 2: Production Execution\n```python\n# Triggered every 30 seconds\n\n# 1. Execute with Selected Engines\nsensor_engine = session.get_engine(\'sensor\')\nactuator_engine = session.get_engine(\'actuator\')\n\n# Read temperature\ntemp = sensor_engine.execute(Action(\n    action_type=ActionType.READ_SENSOR,\n    parameters={\'sensor_id\': \'temp_sensor_1\'}\n))\n\n# Check gate\nif temp < 70:  # Too cold\n    actuator_engine.execute(Action(\n        action_type=ActionType.WRITE_ACTUATOR,\n        parameters={\'actuator_id\': \'hvac_unit_1\', \'command\': \'heat\'}\n    ))\nelif temp > 75:  # Too hot\n    actuator_engine.execute(Action(\n        action_type=ActionType.WRITE_ACTUATOR,\n        parameters={\'actuator_id\': \'hvac_unit_1\', \'command\': \'cool\'}\n    ))\n\n# 3. Produce Deliverables\ndeliverables = {\n    \'temperature_log\': temp,\n    \'action_taken\': \'heat\' if temp < 70 else \'cool\' if temp > 75 else \'none\',\n    \'timestamp\': datetime.now()\n}\n```\n\n## KEY INSIGHTS\n\n### 1. Sessions Are Isolated Control Planes\n- Each session has its own engines\n- Factory session doesn\'t load content engines\n- Blog session doesn\'t load sensor engines\n- Reduces complexity, improves security\n\n### 2. EngineType.API: APIEngine,\n        EngineType.CONTENT: ContentEngine,\n        EngineType.COMMAND: CommandEngine,\n        EngineType.AGENT: AgentEngine,\n    }\n    \n    @classmethod\n    def cls.CONTROL_TYPE_ENGINES.get(control_type, [])\n        engines = []\n        \n        for engine_type in engine_types:\n            engine_class = cls.ENGINE_CLASSES.get(engine_type)\n            if engine_class:\n                engine = engine_class()\n                engines.append(engine)\n                \n        return engines\n\n# ============================================================================\n# SESSION WITH ENGINE ISOLATION\n# ============================================================================\n\nclass IsolatedSession:\n    """\n    Session with isolated engine set\n    Each session loads ONLY the engines it needs\n    """\n    \n    def __init__(self, session_id: str, user_id: str, repository_id: str, control_type: ControlType):\n        self.session_id = session_id\n        self.user_id = user_id\n        self.repository_id = repository_id\n        self.control_type = control_type\n        \n        # Load engines for this control type\n        self.engines: Dict[EngineType, BaseEngine] = {}\n        self._load_engines()\n        \n        # Universal engines (always loaded)\n        self.scheduler = GovernanceScheduler()\n        self.orchestrator = WorkflowOrchestrator()\n        \n        # Execution packet\n        self.packet: Optional[ExecutionPacket] = None\n        \n        # State\n        self.created_at = datetime.now()\n        self.state = \'active\'\n        \n    def _load_engines(self):\n        """Load engines for this session\'s control type"""\n        engines = EngineRegistry.get_engines_for_control_type(self.control_type)\n        \n        for engine in engines:\n            engine.load()\n            self.engines[engine.engine_type] = engine\n            \n        logger.info(f"Session {self.session_id}: Loaded {len(self.engines)} engines for {self.control_type.value}")\n        \n    def get_engine(self, engine_type: EngineType) -> Optional[BaseEngine]:\n        """Get engine by type (only if loaded in this session)"""\n        return self.engines.get(engine_type)\n        \n    def has_engine(self, engine_type: EngineType) -> bool:\n        """Check if engine is loaded in this session"""\n        return engine_type in self.engines\n        \n    def set_packet(self, packet: ExecutionPacket):\n        """Set execution packet for this session"""\n        self.packet = packet\n        \n    def execute_packet(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        """Execute the session\'s packet"""\n        if not self.packet:\n            return {\'error\': \'No packet set\'}\n            \n        # Validate packet can execute\n        can_execute, reasons = self.packet.can_execute()\n        if not can_execute:\n            return {\'error\': \'Cannot execute packet\', \'reasons\': reasons}\n            \n        # Execute each action with appropriate engine\n        results = []\n        for action in self.packet.task_graph:\n            # Find engine for this action type\n            engine = self._get_engine_for_action(action)\n            \n            if not engine:\n                results.append({\n                    \'action_id\': action.action_id,\n                    \'status\': \'failed\',\n                    \'error\': f\'No engine loaded for {action.action_type.value}\'\n                })\n                continue\n                \n            # Execute action\n            try:\n                result = engine.execute(action)\n                results.append({\n                    \'action_id\': action.action_id,\n                    \'status\': \'success\',\n                    \'result\': result\n                })\n            except Exception as e:\n                results.append({\n                    \'action_id\': action.action_id,\n                    \'status\': \'failed\',\n                    \'error\': str(e)\n                })\n                \n        return {\n            \'session_id\': self.session_id,\n            \'packet_id\': self.packet.packet_id,\n            \'results\': results,\n            \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n        }\n        \n    def _get_engine_for_action(self, action: Action) -> Optional[BaseEngine]:\n        """Get the appropriate engine for an action type"""\n        action_to_engine = {\n            ActionType.READ_SENSOR: EngineType.SENSOR,\n            ActionType.WRITE_ACTUATOR: EngineType.ACTUATOR,\n            ActionType.QUERY_DATABASE: EngineType.DATABASE,\n            ActionType.CALL_API: EngineType.API,\n            ActionType.GENERATE_CONTENT: EngineType.CONTENT,\n            ActionType.EXECUTE_COMMAND: EngineType.COMMAND,\n        }\n        \n        engine_type = action_to_engine.get(action.action_type)\n        return self.get_engine(engine_type) if engine_type else None\n        \n    def close(self):\n        """Close session and unload engines"""\n        for engine in self.engines.values():\n            engine.unload()\n        self.state = \'closed\'\n        logger.info(f"Session {self.session_id}: Closed")\n\n# True Universal Control Plane\nSupports ANY automation type:\n- ✅ Factory/IoT (sensors, actuators)\n- ✅ Content/Publishing (generation, APIs)\n- ✅ Data Processing (databases, compute)\n- ✅ System Admin (commands)\n- ✅ Agent Reasoning (swarms)\n\n### 2. Session Isolation\n- Each session has its own engine set\n- Sessions can\'t access each other\'s engines\n- Sessions can communicate via plans\n- Clean separation of concerns\n\n## 📈 System Architecture\n\n```\nANY Automation Request\n  ↓\nUniversalControlPlane\n  ↓\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│ PHASE 1: GENERATIVE SETUP                               │\n│                                                         │\n│ 1.
